\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ file\ implements\ a\ hashtable,\ much\ like\ the\ C++11\ unordered\_set/unordered\_map.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ proposed\ classes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ primary\ distinctions\ between\ this\ hashtable\ and\ C++11\ unordered\ containers\ are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ hashtable\ is\ savvy\ to\ an\ environment\ that\ doesn't\ have\ exception\ handling,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ as\ is\ sometimes\ the\ case\ with\ console\ or\ embedded\ environments.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ hashtable\ is\ slightly\ more\ space-\/efficient\ than\ a\ conventional\ std\ hashtable\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ implementation\ on\ platforms\ with\ 64\ bit\ size\_t.\ \ This\ is\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ because\ std\ STL\ uses\ size\_t\ (64\ bits)\ in\ data\ structures\ whereby\ 32\ bits\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ of\ data\ would\ be\ fine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ hashtable\ can\ contain\ objects\ with\ alignment\ requirements.\ TR1\ hash\ tables\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ cannot\ do\ so\ without\ a\ bit\ of\ tedious\ non-\/portable\ effort.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ hashtable\ supports\ debug\ memory\ naming\ natively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ hashtable\ provides\ a\ find\ function\ that\ lets\ you\ specify\ a\ type\ that\ is\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ different\ from\ the\ hash\ table\ key\ type.\ This\ is\ particularly\ useful\ for\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ the\ storing\ of\ string\ objects\ but\ finding\ them\ by\ char\ pointers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ hashtable\ provides\ a\ lower\ level\ insert\ function\ which\ lets\ the\ caller\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ specify\ the\ hash\ code\ and\ optionally\ the\ node\ instance.}}
